23/02/2020 Ã  15:34 - Ferdinand IMSP: SÃ©minaire dâ€™UnitÃ© de MathÃ©matiques* 


 _Lundi 24 FÃ©vrier 2020_


             15h00


Speaker MAMADOU Pouye


Topic: On structure of quadratic Lie-type superalgebras.


Abstract : we consider a Lie-type superalgebra endowed with a NIS( ie non degenerate, invariant and supersymmetric ) bilinear form. Such superalgebra is called quadratic Lie-type superalgebra.


Quadratic structure has been study for many non associative (super) algebra like Lie (super)algebras, Leibniz (super) algebras, ..... due to its interaction with other properties of the structure considered. In this work, we will investigate quadratic Lie-type superalgebras. In order to do so, we first show that all quadratic LTS are symmetric( which means that simultaneously left and right LTS)  and only abelian LTS can be endowed simultaneously with an odd NIS bilinear form and an even NIS bilinear form.

We introduce representation of LTS and give a necessary and suffisant condition for a LTS to be quadratic by using the adjoint and co-adjoint representation.

We also define the notion of double extension and use it to give an inductive description of non supercommutative LTS ( in other words we show that the study of non supercommutative LTS can be reduce to the one of quadratic supercommutative LTS).

Finally we introduce  the notion of T*-extension for LTS and give necessary and suffisant for a LTS to be express in for of a T*-extension.

*ModÃ©rateur* KABIROU

I write on behalf of the AAU Secretary General to invite you to participate in the celebration of the 2020 African Universities' week which comes off from November 9-13, 2020 by registering via https://tinyurl.com/2020AUWeek.  

 

The African Universitiesâ€™ Week (AU Week) is celebrated annually by universities in Africa to commemorate the birth of the AAU on the 12th November 1967 in Rabat, Morocco and has been celebrated by HEIs since the year 2000.

 

For the first time, one continental virtual weeklong event is planned for the 2020 AU Week Celebrations - instead of various physical events in different African Universities. The rich bouquet of programme lined up for the week include keynote addresses and webinars on various topical issues- including Open Access, Blended Education, Leadership by Women, and Geo-Tourism, among others. The programme will also feature sessions dedicated to AAU members and opportunities for collaborating among themselves and with other institutions.  

 

AAU recommends all stakeholders assist by circulating information concerning the AU Week Celebrations to other stakeholders. to encourage their participation.  Representatives from diverse sectors including â€“ health, agricultural, financial, and educational industries, research institutions and corporate organisations are invited to actively participate in the celebrations.

Dear all,

The next conference will take place on Wednesday, November 25 at 4:00 pm (Paris time).

It will be given by Claude Kirchner, Inria - France by videoconference on the theme Â« Why digital ethics? Â».

when connecting via the link above:

connect with microphone and camera disabled to save bandwidth

your microphones and cameras will be disabled
